    WHERE ((((((([a].[INVMI_Id] = [b].[INVMI_Id]) AND ([b].[INVMT_Id] = [c].[INVMT_Id])) AND ([a].[INVMI_Id] = [d].[INVMI_Id])) AND ([a].[MI_Id] = [c].[MI_Id])) AND ([a].[INVMI_ActiveFlg] = 1)) AND ([b].[INVMIT_ActiveFlg] = 1)) AND ([c].[INVMT_ActiveFlg] = 1)) AND ([a].[INVMI_Id] = @__pi_INVMI_Id_0)
) AS [t]
ORDER BY [t].[INVMT_Id]" (0723d8ff)
